Stockholder: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">You are cordially invited to attend the 2018 Annual Meeting (the &#147;Meeting&#148;) of Goldman Sachs Middle Market Lending
Corp. (the &#147;Company&#148;) to be held on Friday, November&nbsp;2, 2018, at 10:00 a.m. (Eastern time), at&nbsp;the offices of Goldman Sachs Asset Management, L.P., located at 30 Hudson Street, Jersey City, New Jersey 07302. Please note that if
you plan to attend the Meeting in person, photographic identification will be required for admission. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>The meeting is being
held&nbsp;to (i)&nbsp;elect four directors of the Company, who will each serve until the 2019 annual meeting of stockholders and until his or her successor is duly elected and qualified, and (ii)&nbsp;to ratify the selection of
PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP as the Company&#146;s independent registered public accounting firm for the fiscal year ending December&nbsp;31, 2018. </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A formal Notice of Annual Meeting and Proxy Statement setting forth in detail the matters to come before the Meeting are attached hereto, and
a proxy card is enclosed for your use. You should read the Proxy Statement carefully. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>WHETHER OR NOT YOU PLAN TO BE PRESENT AT THE
MEETING, YOUR VOTE IS VERY IMPORTANT.</B> If you do not plan to be present in person at the Meeting, you can vote by signing, dating and returning the enclosed proxy card promptly or by using the Internet or telephone voting options as described on
your proxy card. If you have any questions regarding the proxy materials, please contact the Company at <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(312)&nbsp;655-4702.</FONT> Your prompt response will help reduce proxy solicitation costs&#151;which are paid
by the Company and its stockholders&#151;and will also mean that you can avoid receiving <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">follow-up</FONT> phone calls and mailings. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:54%; text-indent:-2%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sincerely, </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

York 10282 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>NOTICE OF ANNUAL MEETING </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>To Be Held On November&nbsp;2, 2018 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">September&nbsp;6, 2018 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Notice is
hereby given to the owners of shares of common stock (the &#147;Stockholders&#148;) of Goldman Sachs Middle Market Lending Corp. (the &#147;Company&#148;) that: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The 2018 Annual Meeting of Stockholders (the &#147;Meeting&#148;) will be held on Friday, November&nbsp;2, 2018, at 10:00 a.m. (Eastern time),
at the offices of Goldman Sachs Asset Management, L.P., located at 30 Hudson Street, Jersey City, New Jersey 07302, for the following purposes (the &#147;Proposals&#148;): </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>1.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B>to elect four directors of the Company, who will each serve until the 2019 annual meeting of the
stockholders and until his or her successor is duly elected and qualified; and </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>2.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B>to ratify the selection of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP as the Company&#146;s independent registered public
accounting firm for the fiscal year ending December&nbsp;31, 2018. </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The matters referred to above are discussed in
the Proxy Statement attached to this Notice. The Board of Directors of the Company, including each of the independent directors, unanimously recommends that you vote <B>&#147;FOR&#148;</B> the Proposal. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Stockholders of record at the close of business on September&nbsp;5, 2018 are entitled to receive notice of, and to vote at, the Meeting and
at any postponements or adjournments thereof. Each Stockholder is invited to attend the Meeting in person. Please note that if you plan to attend the Meeting in person, photographic identification will be required for admission. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Your vote is extremely important to us. If you will not attend the Meeting in person, we urge you to sign, date and promptly return the
enclosed proxy card in the envelope provided, which is addressed for your convenience and needs no postage if mailed in the United States. You may also vote easily and quickly by Internet or by telephone. In the event there are not sufficient votes
for a quorum or to approve the Proposal at the time of the Meeting, the Meeting may be postponed or adjourned in order to permit further solicitation of proxies by the Company. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:54%; text-indent:-2%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">By Order of the Board of Directors </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:54%; text-indent:-2%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">of Goldman Sachs Middle Market Lending Corp. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>YOUR VOTE IS IMPORTANT </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>NO MATTER HOW MANY SHARES YOU OWN </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">To secure the largest possible representation at the Meeting, please mark your proxy card, sign it, date it, and return it in the postage-paid
envelope provided (unless you are voting by Internet or by telephone). <B>If you sign, date, and return a proxy card but give no voting instructions, your shares will be voted &#147;FOR&#148; all of the proposals indicated on the card.</B> If you
prefer, you may instead vote via the Internet or by telephone. To vote in this manner, you should refer to the directions below. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">To vote
via the Internet, please access the website found on your proxy card and follow the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">on-screen</FONT> instructions on the website. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">To vote by telephone, Stockholders within the United States should call the toll-free number found on the proxy card and follow the recorded
instructions. Stockholders outside the United States should vote via the Internet or by submitting a proxy card instead. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">You may revoke
your proxy at any time at or before the Meeting (1)&nbsp;by notifying the Secretary of the Company in writing at the Company&#146;s principal executive offices, (2)&nbsp;by submitting a properly executed, later-dated proxy or (3)&nbsp;by attending
the Meeting and voting in person. </P>

 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ANNUAL MEETING </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>OF </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>GOLDMAN SACHS MIDDLE
MARKET LENDING CORP. </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">200 West Street </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">New York, New York 10282 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>PROXY
STATEMENT </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">September&nbsp;6, 2018 </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This Proxy Statement is furnished in connection with the solicitation of proxies by and on behalf of the Board of Directors (the
&#147;Board&#148;) of Goldman Sachs Middle Market Lending Corp. (the &#147;Company,&#148; &#147;we,&#148; &#147;our&#148; and &#147;us&#148;) for use at the 2018 Annual Meeting of Stockholders (the &#147;Meeting&#148;), to be held at the offices of
Goldman Sachs Asset Management, L.P., located at 30 Hudson Street, Jersey City, New Jersey 07302, on Friday, November&nbsp;2, 2018, at 10:00&nbsp;a.m. (Eastern time), and any postponement or adjournment thereof. Much of the information in this Proxy
Statement is required under rules of the Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#147;SEC&#148;), and some of it is technical in nature. If there is anything you do not understand, please contact the Company at
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(312)&nbsp;655-4702.</FONT> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This Proxy Statement, the accompanying Notice of Annual Meeting and proxy
card are being mailed to the Company&#146;s stockholders (the &#147;Stockholders&#148;) of record as of September&nbsp;5, 2018 (the &#147;Record Date&#148;) on or about September&nbsp;10, 2018. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>PURPOSE OF THE MEETING </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">At the Meeting, you will be asked to vote on the following proposal: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">To elect four directors of the Company who will each serve until the 2019 annual meeting of the stockholders
and until his or her successor is duly elected and qualified (&#147;Proposal 1&#148;); and </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">2.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">To ratify the selection of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP as the Company&#146;s independent registered public
accounting firm for the fiscal year ending December&nbsp;31, 2018 (&#147;Proposal&nbsp;2&#148;). </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>INFORMATION
REGARDING THIS SOLICITATION </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">It is expected that the solicitation of proxies will be primarily by mail. The Company&#146;s officers,
and personnel of Goldman Sachs Asset Management, L.P. (the &#147;Investment Adviser&#148;), the Company&#146;s Investment Adviser and transfer agent and any authorized proxy solicitation agent, may also solicit proxies by telephone, email,
facsimile, Internet, or in person. If the Company records votes through the Internet or by telephone, it will use procedures designed to authenticate Stockholders&#146; identities to allow Stockholders to authorize the voting of their shares in
accordance with their instructions and to confirm that their identities have been properly recorded. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company will pay the expenses
associated with this Proxy Statement and solicitation, in a manner agreed upon by the Board. The Company has engaged Broadridge Financial Solutions, Inc. (&#147;Broadridge&#148;), an </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">1 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
independent proxy solicitation firm, to assist in the distribution of the proxy materials and tabulation of proxies. The cost of Broadridge&#146;s services with respect to the Company is
estimated to be approximately $48,533, plus reasonable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">out-of-pocket</FONT></FONT> expenses. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">To vote by mail, sign, date, and promptly return the enclosed proxy card in the accompanying postage
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-paid</FONT> envelope. To vote by Internet or telephone, please use the control number on your proxy card and follow the instructions as described on your proxy card. If you have any questions regarding the proxy
materials, please contact the Company at <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(312)&nbsp;655-4702.</FONT> <B>If the enclosed proxy card is properly executed and received prior to the Meeting and has not been revoked, the shares represented thereby will
be voted in accordance with the instructions marked on the returned proxy card or, if no instructions are marked, the proxy card will be voted &#147;FOR&#148; each of the Proposals described in this Proxy Statement; and in the discretion of the
persons named as proxies in connection with any other matter that may properly come before the Meeting or any adjournment(s) or postponement(s) thereof.</B> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Any person giving a proxy may revoke it at any time before it is exercised (1)&nbsp;by notifying the Secretary of the Company in writing at
the Company&#146;s principal executive offices, (2)&nbsp;by submitting a properly executed, later-dated proxy or (3)&nbsp;by attending the Meeting and voting in person. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If (i)&nbsp;you are a member of a household in which multiple Stockholders share the same address, (ii)&nbsp;your shares are held in
&#147;street name&#148; and (iii)&nbsp;your broker or bank has received consent to household material, then your broker or bank may send to your household only one copy of this Proxy Statement, unless your broker or bank previously received contrary
instructions from a Stockholder in your household. If you are part of a household that has received only one copy of this Proxy Statement, the Company will deliver promptly a separate copy of this Proxy Statement to you upon written or oral request.
To receive a separate copy of this Proxy Statement, please contact the Company by calling <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(312)&nbsp;655-4702</FONT> or by mail to the Company&#146;s principal executive offices at Goldman Sachs Middle Market Lending
Corp., 200 West Street, New York, New York 10282. If your shares are held with certain banks, trust companies, brokers, dealers, investment advisers and other financial intermediaries (each, an &#147;Authorized Institution&#148;) and you would like
to receive a separate copy of future proxy statements, notices of internet availability of proxy materials, prospectuses or annual reports or you are now receiving multiple copies of these documents and would like to receive a single copy in the
future, please contact your Authorized Institution. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>IMPORTANT NOTICE REGARDING THE AVAILABILITY OF PROXY MATERIALS FOR THE </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ANNUAL MEETING TO BE HELD ON NOVEMBER&nbsp;2, 2018 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This Proxy Statement is available online at&nbsp;www.proxyvote.com&nbsp;(please have the control number found on your proxy card ready when
you visit this website). </P>

Reporting Compliance </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Pursuant to Section&nbsp;16(a) of the Exchange Act, a company&#146;s directors and executive officers and any
persons holding more than 10% of the company&#146;s common stock are required to report their beneficial ownership and any changes therein to the SEC and the company. Specific due dates for those reports have been established, and a company is
required to report in this proxy statement any failure to file such reports by those due dates. Based on our review of filings with the SEC and written representations furnished to us during 2017, the directors, executive officers and 10% beneficial
owners filed all such reports within the specified time period. </P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>PROPOSAL 1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ELECTION OF DIRECTORS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Prior to the Company listing its common stock on a national securities exchange (an &#147;Exchange Listing&#148;), the Company&#146;s
certificate of incorporation provides that directors will each serve for a one year term. However, immediately prior to an Exchange Listing, the Company&#146;s Board will be divided into three classes, and, at such time, each class of directors will
hold office for a three-year term. Since an Exchange Listing has not occurred, at the Meeting you will be asked to elect four directors to serve until the 2019 annual meeting of stockholders and until his or her successor is duly elected and
qualified, or until his or her earlier death, resignation, removal or disqualification. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Information concerning the nominees and other
relevant factors is provided below. Using the enclosed proxy card or voting by the Internet or by telephone, a Stockholder may vote his or her shares &#147;For&#148; or &#147;Against,&#148; or may abstain from voting with respect to the election of
any nominee. If the enclosed proxy card is properly executed and received prior to the Meeting (and has not been revoked) but no instructions are marked, the proxies will vote &#147;FOR&#148; each of the nominees. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Each of Ms.&nbsp;Katherine (&#147;Kaysie&#148;) Uniacke, and Messrs. Carlos E. Evans, Timothy J. Leach, and Richard A. Mark has consented to
his or her nomination and has agreed to continue to serve if elected. If, at the time of the Meeting, for any reason, any of Ms.&nbsp;Uniacke, or Messrs. Evans, Leach, or Mark is not available for election or is not able to serve as a director, the
persons named as proxies intend to exercise their voting power in favor of such person as is nominated by the Board as a substitute. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>THE BOARD, INCLUDING EACH OF THE INDEPENDENT DIRECTORS, UNANIMOUSLY </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>RECOMMENDS THAT YOU VOTE &#147;FOR&#148; EACH NOMINEE LISTED ABOVE. </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Information about the Director Nominees </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Set forth below are the names of the nominees for director and their addresses, ages, terms of office, principal occupations for at least the
past five years and any other directorships they hold. Director nominees who (1)&nbsp;are not deemed to be &#147;interested persons,&#148; as defined in the 1940 Act, of the Company, (2)&nbsp;meet the definition of &#147;independent directors&#148;
under the corporate governance standards of the New York Stock Exchange (&#147;NYSE&#148;) and (3)&nbsp;meet the independence requirements of Section&nbsp;10A(m)(3) of the Exchange Act are referred to as &#147;Independent Directors.&#148;
Ms.&nbsp;Uniacke is deemed to be an &#147;interested person&#148; of the Company and is referred to as the &#147;Interested Director.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Each of Ms.&nbsp;Uniacke, and Messrs. Evans, Leach, and Mark has been nominated for election as a director to serve until the 2019 annual
meeting of stockholders. None of the nominees are being proposed for election pursuant to any agreement or understanding between such nominee and the Company. </P>

customer contact management services, and is a member of the Board of Directors of Highwoods Properties, Inc., a real estate investment trust, where he serves as chair of the Compensation/Governance Committee and as a member of the Executive
Committee. Prior to his retirement in 2014, Mr.&nbsp;Evans worked for Wells Fargo Bank, most recently serving as executive vice president and group head of the eastern </P>

client assets exceeded $200&nbsp;billion. Before that, Ms.&nbsp;Uniacke was head of GSAM&#146;s Global Cash Services business, where she was responsible for overseeing the management of assets exceeding $100&nbsp;billion. Ms.&nbsp;Uniacke worked at

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Compensation of Directors </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Prior to January&nbsp;1, 2017, each Independent Director was compensated with a unitary annual fee of $75,000 for his or her services as one of
our directors and as a member of the Audit Committee and Governance and Nominating Committee and the director designated as &#147;audit committee financial expert&#148; received an additional $5,000 for his services in such capacity. From
January&nbsp;1, 2017 through June&nbsp;30, 2017, each Independent Director is compensated with a unitary annual fee of $100,000, which increased to $125,000 as of July&nbsp;1, 2017, for his services as one of our directors and as a member of the
Audit Committee and Governance and Nominating Committee. As of January&nbsp;1, 2017, the director designated as &#147;audit committee financial expert&#148; receives an additional $15,000 for his services in such capacity and the Lead Independent
Director receives an additional $25,000 for his services in such capacity. As of December 2017, the role of Lead Independent Director transitioned to Independent Chairman of the Board of Directors. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Independent Directors of the Board of Directors and each committee are also reimbursed for travel and other expenses incurred in
connection with attending meetings. We may also pay the incidental costs of a director to attend training or other types of conferences relating to the business development company industry. </P>

term is defined in the Investment Company Act. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Board Composition and Leadership Structure </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company was formed on June&nbsp;13, 2016 and effective January&nbsp;30, 2017, converted from Goldman Sachs Middle Market Lending LLC, a
Delaware limited liability company, into Goldman Sachs Middle Market Lending Corp., a Delaware corporation. As a result, any references in this section to meetings of the Company&#146;s Board prior to January&nbsp;30, 2017 refer to meetings of the
Company&#146;s LLC predecessor. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company&#146;s business and affairs are managed under the direction of its Board. The Board consists
of four members, three of whom are Independent Directors. &#147;Independent Directors&#148; are directors who (1)&nbsp;are not deemed to be &#147;interested persons,&#148; of the Company (as defined in the Investment Company Act), (2) meet the
definition of &#147;independent directors&#148; under the corporate governance standards of the NYSE and (3)&nbsp;meet the independence requirements of Section&nbsp;10A(m)(3) of the Exchange Act. The Board elects our officers, who serve
</P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">9 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
at the discretion of the Board of Directors. The responsibilities of the Board include quarterly valuation of our assets, corporate governance activities, oversight of our financing arrangements
and oversight of our investment activities. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Board&#146;s role in the management of the Company is one of oversight. Oversight of our
investment activities extends to oversight of the risk management processes employed by our Investment Adviser as part of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">its&nbsp;day-to-day</FONT></FONT> management of our
investment activities. The Board reviews risk management processes at both regular and special Board meetings throughout the year, consulting with appropriate representatives of our Investment Adviser as necessary and periodically requesting the
production of risk management reports or presentations. The goal of the Board&#146;s risk oversight function is to ensure that the risks associated with our investment activities are accurately identified, thoroughly investigated and responsibly
addressed. The Board&#146;s oversight function cannot, however, eliminate all risks or ensure that particular events do not adversely affect the value of the investments held by the Company. The Board also has primary responsibility for the
valuation of our assets. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Board has established an Audit Committee, Governance and Nominating Committee (the &#147;Governance and
Nominating Committee&#148;), Compliance Committee (the &#147;Compliance Committee&#148;), and Contract Review Committee (the &#147;Contract Review Committee&#148;). The scope of each committee&#146;s responsibilities is discussed in greater detail
below. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Timothy J. Leach, an Independent Director, serves as Chairman of the Board. The Board believes that it is in the best interests of
the Company for Mr.&nbsp;Leach to lead the Board because of his familiarity with the Company&#146;s portfolio companies, his broad corporate background and experience with financial and investment matters and his significant senior management
experience, as described above. Mr.&nbsp;Leach generally acts as a liaison between the Company&#146;s management, officers and attorneys between meetings of the Board and generally presides over all executive sessions of the Independent Directors
without management. The Board believes that its leadership structure is appropriate because the structure allocates areas of responsibility among the individual directors and the committees in a manner that enhances effective oversight. The Board
also believes that its size creates an efficient corporate governance structure that provides opportunity for direct communication and interaction between management and the Board. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Board of Directors had ten formal meetings in 2017. Each director nominee that was a member of the Board during the fiscal year ended
December&nbsp;31, 2017 attended 100% of the aggregate number of meetings of the Board and of the respective committees on which he or she served. To promote effectiveness of the Board, directors are strongly encouraged to attend regularly scheduled
Board meetings in person. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">None of the director nominees attended the 2017 annual meeting. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Committees of the Board of Directors </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Audit
Committee </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The members of the Audit Committee are Carlos E. Evans, Timothy J. Leach, and Richard A. Mark, each of whom is an
Independent Director and meets the current independence and experience requirements of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Rule&nbsp;10A-3&nbsp;of</FONT> the Exchange Act and none of whom is an &#147;interested person&#148; of the Company as defined in
Section&nbsp;2(a)(19) of the Investment Company Act. Richard A. Mark serves as Chairman of the Audit Committee. The Board and the Audit Committee have determined that Richard A. Mark is an &#147;audit committee financial expert,&#148; as defined in
Item 407 of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Regulation&nbsp;S-K&nbsp;under</FONT> the Exchange Act. The Audit Committee is responsible for overseeing matters relating to the appointment and activities of the Company&#146;s auditors, audit plans and
procedures, various accounting and financial reporting issues and changes in accounting policies, and reviewing the results and scope of the audit and other services provided by the Company&#146;s independent public accountants. The Audit Committee
is also responsible for aiding the Board in fair value pricing debt and equity securities that are not publicly traded or for which current market values are not readily available. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit Committee held five formal meetings in 2017. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">10 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Governance and Nominating Committee </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Governance and Nominating Committee members are Kaysie Uniacke, Carlos E. Evans, Richard A. Mark and Timothy J. Leach. Kaysie Uniacke
serves as the Chairman of the Governance and Nominating Committee. The Governance and Nominating Committee is responsible for identifying, researching and nominating Independent Directors for election by the Company&#146;s stockholders, when
necessary, selecting nominees to fill vacancies on the Board or a committee of the Board, developing and recommending to the Board a set of corporate governance principles and overseeing the evaluation of the Board and the Company&#146;s management.
The Governance and Nominating Committee will consider nominees recommended by the Company&#146;s stockholders that are properly submitted in accordance with the Company&#146;s bylaws. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Governance and Nominating Committee held four formal meetings in 2017. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Compliance Committee </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The
Compliance Committee members are Kaysie Uniacke, Carlos E. Evans, Richard A. Mark and Timothy J. Leach. Kaysie Uniacke serves as Chairman of the Compliance Committee. The Compliance Committee is responsible for overseeing the Company&#146;s
compliance processes, and, insofar as they relate to services provided to us, the compliance processes of the Company&#146;s Investment Adviser, principal underwriters, administrator and transfer agent, except that compliance processes relating to
the accounting and financial reporting processes and certain related matters are overseen by the Audit Committee. In addition, the Compliance Committee provides assistance to the full Board with respect to compliance matters. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Compliance Committee held five formal meetings in 2017. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Contract Review Committee </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The
Contract Review Committee members are Kaysie Uniacke, Carlos E. Evans, Richard A. Mark and Timothy J. Leach. Kaysie Uniacke serves as Chairman of the Contract Review Committee. The Contract Review Committee is responsible for overseeing the
processes of the Board for reviewing and monitoring performance under the Company&#146;s investment management, placement agency, underwriting (if any), transfer agency and certain other agreements with the Company&#146;s Investment Adviser and its
affiliates. The Contract Review Committee provides appropriate assistance to the Board in connection with the Board&#146;s approval, oversight and review of the Company&#146;s other service providers, including the Company&#146;s
custodian/accounting <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">agent,&nbsp;sub-transfer&nbsp;agents,</FONT> placement agent, professional (legal and accounting) firms and printing firms. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Contract Review Committee had one formal meeting in 2017. </P>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">11 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The address for each executive officer is c/o Goldman Sachs Asset Management, L.P., 200 West
Street, New York, New York 10282. Each officer holds office at the pleasure of the Board until the next election of officers or until his or her successor is duly elected and qualifies. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Brendan McGovern.</B> Mr.&nbsp;McGovern has served as chief executive officer and president of the Company since June 2016.
Mr.&nbsp;McGovern heads GSAM&#146;s Private Credit Group, is chief executive officer and president of GS BDC and GS PMMC and also serves <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">as&nbsp;co-head&nbsp;and</FONT> senior portfolio manager of the GSAM Credit
Alternatives portfolio management team. He is also the Chair and a voting member of the Private Credit Group&#146;s Investment Committee, which is responsible for evaluating and approving all of the Company&#146;s investments. Mr.&nbsp;McGovern
joined the firm in 2006. Prior to joining the firm, Mr.&nbsp;McGovern served as a managing director in the Global Investment Group at Amaranth Advisors, where <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">he&nbsp;co-headed&nbsp;the</FONT> fund&#146;s private
placement efforts for both debt and equity linked products in the United States. He is also on the board of directors for the Oxalosis and Hyperoxaluria Foundation. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Jon Yoder.</B> Mr.&nbsp;Yoder has served as chief operating officer of the Company since June 2016. Mr.&nbsp;Yoder is chief operating
officer of GS BDC and GS PMMC and a member of GSAM&#146;s Private Credit Group with a focus on sourcing, structuring and executing privately negotiated debt financings. He is also a voting member of the Private Credit Group&#146;s Investment
Committee, which is responsible for evaluating and approving all of the Company&#146;s investments. Mr.&nbsp;Yoder joined the firm in 2005. Prior to joining the firm, he was a member of the mergers and acquisitions and private equity groups at Paul,
Weiss, Rifkind, Wharton&nbsp;&amp; Garrison, LLP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Jonathan Lamm.</B> Mr.&nbsp;Lamm has served as chief financial officer and treasurer
of the Company since June 2016. Mr.&nbsp;Lamm is also chief financial officer and treasurer of GS BDC and GS PMMC and chief operating officer of the GSAM Credit Alternatives portfolio management team, responsible for the operations of the business,
including business financials, infrastructure support, and IT project management, as well as the continuous improvement of the control environment. Mr.&nbsp;Lamm is secretary and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">a&nbsp;non-voting&nbsp;member</FONT>
of the Private Credit Group&#146;s Investment Committee, which is responsible for evaluating and approving all of the Company&#146;s investments. He joined the firm in 2002. Prior to joining the firm, Mr.&nbsp;Lamm worked in the securities audit
practice at Deloitte&nbsp;&amp; Touche, LLP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Maya Teufel.</B> Ms.&nbsp;Teufel was appointed as chief compliance officer of the Company
in December 2016. Ms.&nbsp;Teufel is currently the chief compliance officer of GS BDC and GS PMMC. Ms.&nbsp;Teufel was the Chief Compliance Officer of Goldman Sachs Trust II from September 2016 to August 2018. Prior to joining GSAM in September
2016, she was, from November 2013 to August 2016, the General Counsel and Chief Compliance Officer of Emerging Global Advisors, LLC (currently part of Ameriprise Financial). While at Emerging Global Advisors, Ms.&nbsp;Teufel also held the position
of fund chief compliance officer from October 2015 to August 2016. Prior to joining Emerging Global Advisors, she was, from July 2005 to November 2013, Vice President, Corporate Counsel at Prudential Insurance Company of America, a subsidiary of
Prudential Financial Inc., an insurance and financial services company. Prior to Prudential, Ms.&nbsp;Teufel was an associate in the mergers and acquisitions groups of Sullivan &amp; Cromwell LLP and Gibson, Dunn &amp; Crutcher LLP. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Salvatore Lentini.</B> Mr.&nbsp;Lentini has served as an executive vice president of the Company since June 2016. Mr.&nbsp;Lentini is
executive vice president of GS BDC and GS PMMC <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">and&nbsp;co-head&nbsp;and</FONT> senior portfolio manager of the GSAM Credit Alternatives investment team and also serves as its head of liquid credit and trading.
Mr.&nbsp;Lentini is also a voting member of Private Credit Group&#146;s Investment Committee, which is responsible for evaluating and approving all of the Company&#146;s investments. Mr.&nbsp;Lentini joined the firm in 2006. Prior to joining the
firm, Mr.&nbsp;Lentini was a managing director in the Global Investments Group at Amaranth Advisors, where he was responsible for trading all credit products within the United States. Before joining Amaranth, he was responsible for trading high
yield and crossover debt at the Royal Bank of Scotland (RBS). Earlier, Mr.&nbsp;Lentini traded high yield fixed income for PaineWebber. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>David Yu.</B> Mr.&nbsp;Yu has served as an executive vice president and Head of Research of the Company since June 2016. Mr.&nbsp;Yu is
executive vice president of GS BDC and GS PMMC and a member of the GSAM Private </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">12 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
Credit Group with a focus on sourcing, structuring and executing privately negotiated debt financings and serves as its Head of Research. Mr.&nbsp;Yu is a voting member of the Private Credit
Group&#146;s Investment Committee, which is responsible for evaluating and approving all of the Company&#146;s investments. Mr.&nbsp;Yu joined the firm in 2006. Prior to joining the firm, Mr.&nbsp;Yu was an associate in the Global Investments Group
at Amaranth Advisors, where he similarly worked with public and private issuers to structure and execute debt and equity financings. Prior to joining Amaranth, he worked in the Leveraged Finance and Sponsor Coverage Group at CIBC World Markets. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Jordan Walter.</B> Mr.&nbsp;Walter has served as an executive vice president of the Company since March 2018. Mr.&nbsp;Walter is a member
of the GSAM Credit Alternatives team with a focus on sourcing and origination of privately negotiated debt financings. Prior to joining GSAM Credit Alternatives, Mr.&nbsp;Walter was a vice president at MCG Capital where he <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-originated</FONT> and managed the security and underwriting strategy for debt and equity financings. Mr.&nbsp;Walter earned a BS in Finance from the Virginia Polytechnic Institution and State University. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Carmine Rossetti.</B> Mr.&nbsp;Rossetti has served as principal accounting officer of the Company since May 2017. Mr.&nbsp;Rossetti is also
the principal accounting officer of GS BDC and GS PMMC. He is a Vice President in the Finance Division of Goldman Sachs&nbsp;&amp; Co. LLC and head of the GSAM Hedge Fund and BDC Controllers teams. Mr.&nbsp;Rossetti is responsible for fund
accounting and financial reporting oversight as well as the continuous improvement of the control environment. Mr.&nbsp;Rossetti joined Goldman Sachs&nbsp;&amp; Co. LLC in 2004. Prior to joining Goldman Sachs&nbsp;&amp; Co. LLC, he worked in the
audit practice at Ernst&nbsp;&amp; Young LLP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Certain Relationships and Related Party Transactions </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Investment Management and Advisory Agreement </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company is party to an investment management agreement, pursuant to which the Company pays GSAM, a wholly owned subsidiary of GS Group
Inc., a quarterly fee for investment management services equal to 0.375% (i.e., an annual rate of 1.50%) of our average NAV (including uninvested cash and cash equivalents), and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">two-part</FONT> incentive fee based
on (a)&nbsp;the amount by which our ordinary income exceeds certain &#147;hurdle rates,&#148; and (b)&nbsp;our capital gains. Certain of the Company&#146;s officers are also officers and employees of GSAM. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the period from January&nbsp;11, 2017 (commencement of operations) to December&nbsp;31, 2017, the Company paid GSAM a total of
$1.74&nbsp;million in fees (excluding fees that are accrued but not paid) pursuant to the Investment Management Agreement, which consisted of $1.74&nbsp;million in management fees and $0.00 in incentive fees. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>License Agreement </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company is
party to a license agreement with an affiliate of Goldman Sachs pursuant to which the Company has been granted <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">a&nbsp;non-exclusive,&nbsp;royalty-free</FONT> license to use the &#147;Goldman Sachs&#148; name. Under
this agreement, the Company shall not have a right to use the Goldman Sachs name if GSAM or another affiliate of Goldman Sachs is not the Company&#146;s Investment Adviser or if the Company&#146;s continued use of such license results in a violation
of applicable law, results in a regulatory burden or has adverse regulatory consequences. Other than with respect to this limited license, the Company has no legal right to the &#147;Goldman Sachs&#148; name. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Investment</FONT> Opportunities </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company has in the past <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-invested,</FONT> and in the future may
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-invest,</FONT> on a concurrent basis with other funds managed by GSAM and its affiliates, but not if such <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-investment</FONT> is impermissible under existing regulatory guidance,
applicable regulations or GSAM&#146;s allocation procedures. Certain types of negotiated <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-investments</FONT> may be made only if the Company receives an order from the SEC permitting the Company to do so. On
January&nbsp;4, 2017, the SEC granted the Company, GS PMMC and GS BDC, as well as certain other funds managed by GSAM in the future, the exemptive relief to make negotiated <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-investments,</FONT> subject to certain
terms and conditions in the exemptive relief. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">13 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Transfer Agent Agreement </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company has entered into a transfer agency agreement (the &#147;Transfer Agency Agreement&#148;), with Goldman Sachs&nbsp;&amp; Co. LLC, an
affiliate of GSAM, pursuant to which Goldman Sachs&nbsp;&amp; Co. LLC, serves as the Company&#146;s transfer agent (&#147;Transfer Agent&#148;), registrar and disbursing agent. The Company pays the Transfer Agent fees at an annual rate of 0.12% of
the average NAV of the Company at the end of the then-current quarter and the prior calendar quarter (and, in the case of the Company&#146;s first quarter, the Company&#146;s NAV as of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">such&nbsp;quarter-end).</FONT>
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the period from January&nbsp;11, 2017 (commencement of operations) to December&nbsp;31, 2017, the Company paid Goldman
Sachs&nbsp;&amp; Co. LLC a total of $0.16&nbsp;million in fees pursuant to the Transfer Agent Agreement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Placement Agent Agreements </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company has entered into an agreement with each of Goldman Sachs&nbsp;&amp; Co. LLC and Goldman Sachs International (each, a
&#147;Placement Agent&#148; and together with various <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-placement</FONT> agents, the &#147;Placement Agents&#148;) pursuant to which the Placement Agents will assist the Company in conducting private placement
offerings. The Placement Agents have entered into or will enter <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">into&nbsp;sub-placement&nbsp;agreements</FONT> (together with the agreements with Goldman Sachs&nbsp;&amp; Co. LLC and Goldman Sachs International, the
&#147;Placement Agent Agreements&#148;) with <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">various&nbsp;sub-placement&nbsp;agents</FONT> to assist in conducting the private placement offering. The Placement Agents are not expected to be compensated by the
Company for their services, but may charge investors a placement fee with respect to their investment in the Company. The Placement Agents may also be compensated by the Investment Adviser, in its discretion, for certain services including
promotional and marketing support, shareholder servicing, operational and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">recordkeeping,&nbsp;sub-accounting,&nbsp;networking</FONT> or administrative services. These payments are made out of the Investment
Adviser&#146;s own resources and/or assets, including from the revenues or profits derived from the advisory fees the Investment Adviser receives from the Company. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Related Party Transaction Review Policy </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit Committee conducts quarterly reviews of any potential related party transactions brought to its attention and, during these reviews,
it also considers any conflicts of interest brought to its attention pursuant to the Company&#146;s Code of Ethics. Each of the Company&#146;s directors and executive officers is instructed and periodically reminded to inform GSAM Compliance of any
potential related party transactions. In addition, each such director and executive officer completes a questionnaire on an annual basis designed to elicit information about any potential related party transactions. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Proxy Voting by the Investment Adviser </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our Investment Adviser has implemented processes designed to prevent conflicts of interest from influencing proxy voting decisions that it
makes on behalf of advisory clients, including us, and to help ensure that such decisions are made in accordance with its fiduciary obligations to its clients. Notwithstanding such proxy voting processes, proxy voting decisions made by our
Investment Adviser with respect to securities held by us may benefit the interests of Goldman Sachs and Accounts other than us. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">14 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>PROPOSAL 2 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>RATIFICATION OF SELECTION OF INDEPENDENT REGISTERED PUBLIC ACCOUNTING FIRM </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">At a meeting of the Board held on December&nbsp;12, 2017, the Audit Committee selected and recommended, and the Board, including a majority of
the Independent Directors, approved, the selection of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP to act as the independent registered public accounting firm for the Company for the fiscal year ending December&nbsp;31, 2018. This selection is presented for
ratification by the Stockholders. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Representatives of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP are expected to be present at the Meeting and will be
available to respond to appropriate questions from Stockholders if necessary. Representatives of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP will be given the opportunity to make statements at the Meeting, if they so desire. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Audit Fees </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The aggregate audit
fees billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2017 were $260,000. No audit fees were billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2016. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fees included in the audit fees category are those associated with the annual audits of financial statements, review of the financial
statements included in the Company&#146;s Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-Qs,</FONT> the filing of the Company&#146;s Registration Statement on Form 10 and services that are normally provided in connection with statutory and regulatory
filings. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Audit-Related Fees </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">No audit-related fees were billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2017 and December&nbsp;31, 2016. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Audit-related fees are for any services rendered to the Company that are reasonably related to the performance of the audits or reviews of the
Company&#146;s financial statements (but not reported as audit fees above). These services include attestation services that are not required by statute or regulation and consultations concerning financial accounting and reporting standards. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The aggregate audit-related fees billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP to GSAM, and any entity controlling, controlled by, or under common
control with, GSAM, that provides ongoing services to the Company, for engagements directly related to the Company&#146;s operations and financial reporting, for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2017 were $1,133,433. These amounts represent fees
PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP billed to GSAM for services related to the SSAE 16 report. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">No audit-related fees were billed by
PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP to GSAM, and any entity controlling, controlled by, or under common control with, GSAM, that provides ongoing services to the Company, for engagements directly related to the Company&#146;s operations and financial
reporting, for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2016. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Tax Fees </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The aggregate fees billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for services rendered to the Company for tax compliance, tax advice and tax planning
for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2017 were $12,500. No fees were billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for services rendered to the Company for tax compliance, tax advice and tax planning for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2016. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">15 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fees included in the tax fees category comprise all services performed by professional staff in
the independent registered public accountant&#146;s tax division except those services related to the audits. This category comprises fees for tax compliance services provided in connection with the preparation and review of the Company&#146;s tax
returns. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>All Other Fees </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">No
fees were billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for products and services provided to the Company, other than the services reported in &#147;Audit Fees,&#148; &#147;Audit Related Fees,&#148; and &#147;Tax Fees&#148; above, for the years ended
December&nbsp;31, 2017 and December&nbsp;31, 2016. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">No other fees were billed by the Company&#146;s independent registered public
accountant to GSAM, and any entity controlling, controlled by, or under common control with, GSAM, that provides ongoing services to the Company, for engagements directly related to the Company&#146;s operations and financial reporting, for the
years ended December&nbsp;31, 2017 and December&nbsp;31, 2016. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Aggregate <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Audit</FONT> Fees </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">No <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> fees were billed to GSAM and service affiliates by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2017 and December&nbsp;31, 2016. This includes any <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services required to be
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approved</FONT> or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services that did not require <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval</FONT> since they did not directly relate to the Company&#146;s
operations or financial reporting. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Pre-Approval</FONT> of Audit and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Audit</FONT>
Services Provided to the Company </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Audit</FONT> Services <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Pre-Approval</FONT> Policy (the &#147;Policy&#148;) adopted by the Audit Committee sets forth the procedures and the conditions pursuant to which services performed by an independent auditor for the Company may be <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approved.</FONT> Services may be <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approved</FONT> specifically by the Audit Committee as a whole or, in certain circumstances, by the Audit Committee Chairman or the person
designated as the audit committee financial expert. In addition, subject to specified cost limitations, certain services may be <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approved</FONT> under the provisions of the Policy. The Policy provides that the
Audit Committee will consider whether the services provided by an independent auditor are consistent with the SEC&#146;s rules on auditor independence. The Policy provides for periodic review and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval</FONT>
by the Audit Committee of the services that may be provided by the independent auditor. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>De Minimis Waiver.</I> The <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval</FONT> requirements of the Policy may be waived with respect to the provision of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services that are permissible for an independent auditor to perform, provided
(1)&nbsp;the aggregate amount of all such services provided constitutes no more than five percent of the total amount of revenues subject to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval</FONT> that was paid to the independent auditors during the
fiscal year in which the services are provided; (2)&nbsp;such services were not recognized by the Company at the time of the engagement to be <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services; and (3)&nbsp;such services are promptly brought
to the attention of the Audit Committee and approved prior to the completion of the audit by the Audit Committee or by one or more members of the Audit Committee to whom authority to grant such approvals has been delegated by the Audit Committee,
pursuant to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval</FONT> provisions of the Policy. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Pre-Approval</FONT> of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Audit</FONT> Services Provided to GSAM.</I>
The Policy provides that, in addition to requiring <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval</FONT> of audit and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services provided to the Company, the Audit Committee will <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approve</FONT> those <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services provided to the Company&#146;s investment adviser (and entities controlling, controlled by or under common control with the investment
adviser that provide ongoing services to the Company) where the engagement relates directly to the operations or financial reporting of the Company. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit Committee has considered these fees and the nature of the services rendered, and has concluded that they are compatible with
maintaining the independence of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP. The Audit </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">16 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
Committee did not approve any of the audit-related, tax, or other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> fees described above pursuant to the&nbsp;&#147;<I>de minimis</I>
exceptions&#148; set forth in Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-01(c)(7)(i)(C)</FONT> and Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-01(c)(7)(ii)</FONT> of Regulation <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">S-X.</FONT> PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP did not
provide any audit-related services, tax services or other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services to GSAM or any entity controlling, controlled by or under common control with GSAM that provides ongoing services to the Company
that the Audit Committee was required to approve pursuant to Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-01(c)(7)(ii)</FONT> of Regulation <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">S-X.</FONT> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>THE BOARD, INCLUDING EACH OF THE INDEPENDENT DIRECTORS, UNANIMOUSLY RECOMMENDS THAT YOU VOTE &#147;FOR&#148; THE RATIFICATION OF
PRICEWATERHOUSECOOPERS LLP AS INDEPENDENT REGISTERED PUBLIC ACCOUNTING FIRM TO THE COMPANY FOR THE FISCAL YEAR ENDING DECEMBER&nbsp;31, 2018. </B></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">17 </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B></B><B><I>Audit Committee Report</I></B><B>
<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">(1)</SUP> </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following is the report of the Audit Committee of Goldman Sachs Middle
Market Lending Corp. (the &#147;Company&#148;) with respect to the Company&#146;s audited financial statements as of December&nbsp;31, 2017 (the &#147;Audited Financial Statements&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit Committee has: (a)&nbsp;reviewed and discussed the Audited Financial Statements with the management of the Company;
(b)&nbsp;discussed with the independent auditor the matters required to be discussed by the Public Company Accounting Oversight Board (&#147;PCAOB&#148;) Standard No.&nbsp;1301, as modified or supplemented; and (c)&nbsp;received the written
disclosures and the letter from the independent auditor required by applicable requirements of the PCAOB Ethics and Independence Rule 3526 regarding the independent auditor&#146;s communications with the Audit Committee concerning independence, and
has discussed with the independent auditor the auditor&#146;s independence. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The members of the Audit Committee are not, and do not
represent themselves to be, professionally engaged in the practice of auditing or accounting and are not employed by the Company for accounting, financial management or internal control purposes. Moreover, the Audit Committee relies on and makes no
independent verification of the facts presented to it or representations made by management or the Company&#146;s independent auditor. Accordingly, the Audit Committee&#146;s oversight does not provide an independent basis to determine that
management has maintained appropriate accounting and/or financial reporting principles and policies, or internal controls and procedures designed to assure compliance with accounting standards and applicable laws and regulations. Furthermore, the
Audit Committee&#146;s considerations and discussions referred to above do not provide assurance that the audit of the Company&#146;s financial statements has been carried out in accordance with the standards of the PCAOB or that the financial
statements are presented in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Based on its consideration of the Audited Financial
Statements and the discussions referred to above with management and the Company&#146;s independent auditor, and subject to the limitations on the responsibilities and role of the Audit Committee set forth in the charter and those discussed above,
the Audit Committee recommended to the Board of Directors that the Audited Financial Statements be accepted by the Board of Directors and included in the Company&#146;s Annual Report on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-K</FONT> for the last
fiscal year for filing with the SEC. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">August&nbsp;1, 2018 </P>
